code: async def forward(self, taskInfo, extra_info):
    from collections import Counter
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []

    # Sub-task 1: Extract and define trip parameters
    cot_instruction = "Sub-task 1: Extract and define the trip parameters from the query."
    cot_agent = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent([taskInfo], extra_info, cot_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, sub-task 1, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")

    # Sub-task 2: Research transportation options
    cot_sc_instruction = "Sub-task 2: Based on the output of sub-task 1, research transportation options, avoiding self-driving."
    N = 3
    cot_agents = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    thinking_mapping = {}
    answer_mapping = {}
    possible_answers = []
    for i in range(N):
        thinking, answer = await cot_agents[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, cot_sc_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents[i].id}, sub-task 2, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
        possible_answers.append(answer.content)
        thinking_mapping[answer.content] = thinking
        answer_mapping[answer.content] = answer
    answer2 = Counter(possible_answers).most_common(1)[0][0]
    thinking2 = thinking_mapping[answer2]
    answer2 = answer_mapping[answer2]
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")

    # Sub-task 3.2.1: Identify potential accommodations in New York
    cot_instruction = "Sub-task 3.2.1: Identify potential accommodations in New York that can accommodate 7 people."
    thinking3_2_1, answer3_2_1 = await cot_agent([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, cot_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3.2.1 output: thinking - {thinking3_2_1.content}; answer - {answer3_2_1.content}")
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, sub-task 3.2.1, thinking: {thinking3_2_1.content}; answer: {answer3_2_1.content}")

    # Sub-task 3.2.2: Evaluate accommodations based on group size and budget
    cot_reflect_instruction = "Sub-task 3.2.2: Based on the output of sub-task 3.2.1, evaluate accommodations based on group size and budget."
    cot_agent = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max = 3
    cot_inputs = [taskInfo, thinking3_2_1, answer3_2_1]
    thinking3_2_2, answer3_2_2 = await cot_agent(cot_inputs, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, sub-task 3.2.2, thinking: {thinking3_2_2.content}; answer: {answer3_2_2.content}")
    for i in range(N_max):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent([taskInfo, thinking3_2_2, answer3_2_2], extra_info, "Sub-task 3.2.2: Provide feedback on accommodation evaluation.", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent.id}, sub-task 3.2.2, feedback: {feedback.content}; correct: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs.extend([thinking3_2_2, answer3_2_2, feedback])
        thinking3_2_2, answer3_2_2 = await cot_agent(cot_inputs, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, sub-task 3.2.2, thinking: {thinking3_2_2.content}; answer: {answer3_2_2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3.2.2 output: thinking - {thinking3_2_2.content}; answer - {answer3_2_2.content}")

    # Sub-task 4: Research attractions
    debate_instruction = "Sub-task 4: Based on the output of sub-task 1, research attractions in each city."
    debate_agents = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Debate Agent', model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in ['Explorer', 'Historian', 'Cultural Enthusiast']]
    max_round = 2
    all_thinking = [[] for _ in range(max_round)]
    all_answer = [[] for _ in range(max_round)]
    for r in range(max_round):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents):
            if r == 0:
                thinking, answer = await agent([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, debate_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1] + all_thinking[r-1]
                thinking, answer = await agent(input_infos, extra_info, debate_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
            all_thinking[r].append(thinking)
            all_answer[r].append(answer)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, sub-task 4, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
    final_decision_agent = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Final Decision Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking4, answer4 = await final_decision_agent([taskInfo] + all_thinking[-1] + all_answer[-1], extra_info, "Sub-task 4: Based on debate outputs, finalize attractions.", is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, sub-task 4, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")

    # Sub-task 5: Research dining options
    debate_instruction = "Sub-task 5: Based on the output of sub-task 1, research dining options in each city."
    all_thinking = [[] for _ in range(max_round)]
    all_answer = [[] for _ in range(max_round)]
    for r in range(max_round):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents):
            if r == 0:
                thinking, answer = await agent([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, debate_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1] + all_thinking[r-1]
                thinking, answer = await agent(input_infos, extra_info, debate_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
            all_thinking[r].append(thinking)
            all_answer[r].append(answer)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, sub-task 5, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
    thinking5, answer5 = await final_decision_agent([taskInfo] + all_thinking[-1] + all_answer[-1], extra_info, "Sub-task 5: Based on debate outputs, finalize dining options.", is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, sub-task 5, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}")

    # Sub-task 6.1.2.1.1: Calculate transportation costs
    cot_reflect_instruction = "Sub-task 6.1.2.1.1: Based on outputs from sub-tasks 2, calculate transportation costs."
    cot_inputs = [taskInfo, thinking2, answer2]
    thinking6_1_2_1_1, answer6_1_2_1_1 = await cot_agent(cot_inputs, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, sub-task 6.1.2.1.1, thinking: {thinking6_1_2_1_1.content}; answer: {answer6_1_2_1_1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 6.1.2.1.1 output: thinking - {thinking6_1_2_1_1.content}; answer - {answer6_1_2_1_1.content}")

    # Sub-task 6.1.2.1.2: Calculate accommodation and dining costs
    cot_reflect_instruction = "Sub-task 6.1.2.1.2: Based on outputs from sub-tasks 3, 4, and 5, calculate accommodation and dining costs."
    cot_inputs = [taskInfo, thinking3_2_2, answer3_2_2, thinking4, answer4, thinking5, answer5]
    thinking6_1_2_1_2, answer6_1_2_1_2 = await cot_agent(cot_inputs, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, sub-task 6.1.2.1.2, thinking: {thinking6_1_2_1_2.content}; answer: {answer6_1_2_1_2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 6.1.2.1.2 output: thinking - {thinking6_1_2_1_2.content}; answer - {answer6_1_2_1_2.content}")

    # Sub-task 6.1.2.2: Adjust itinerary to fit budget
    critic_agent = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_instruction = "Sub-task 6.1.2.2: Provide feedback on the estimated trip cost and adjust the itinerary to fit the budget."
    N_max = 3
    for i in range(N_max):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent([taskInfo, thinking6_1_2_1_1, answer6_1_2_1_1, thinking6_1_2_1_2, answer6_1_2_1_2], extra_info, critic_instruction, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent.id}, sub-task 6.1.2.2, feedback: {feedback.content}; correct: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs.extend([thinking6_1_2_1_1, answer6_1_2_1_1, thinking6_1_2_1_2, answer6_1_2_1_2, feedback])
        thinking6_1_2_1_1, answer6_1_2_1_1 = await cot_agent(cot_inputs, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, sub-task 6.1.2.2, thinking: {thinking6_1_2_1_1.content}; answer: {answer6_1_2_1_1.content}")

                thinking, answer = await agent([taskInfo, thinking6_1_2_1_1, answer6_1_2_1_1, thinking6_1_2_1_2, answer6_1_2_1_2], extra_info, cot_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos = [taskInfo, thinking6_1_2_1_1, answer6_1_2_1_1, thinking6_1_2_1_2, answer6_1_2_1_2] + all_thinking[r-1]
                thinking, answer = await agent(input_infos, extra_info, cot_instruction, is_sub_task=True)
            all_thinking[r].append(thinking)
            all_answer[r].append(answer)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, sub-task 7, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
    final_decision_agent = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Final Decision Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking7, answer7 = await final_decision_agent([taskInfo] + all_thinking[-1] + all_answer[-1], extra_info, "Sub-task 7: Based on debate outputs, finalize the travel plan.", is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, sub-task 7, thinking: {thinking7.content}; answer: {answer7.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 7 output: thinking - {thinking7.content}; answer - {answer7.content}")

    final_answer = self.make_final_answer(thinking7, answer7, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer
